# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes sig-node Kubelet Component Ownership Map

## Your Task

Map the major kubelet components in kubernetes/kubernetes owned by sig-node. Find the Go source files that implement: the pod lifecycle manager, the container runtime interface (CRI) client, the volume manager, and the device plugin manager.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

Perfect! I've successfully created the mapping of the major kubelet components owned by sig-node. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Kubelet Components Owned by sig-node (v1.32.0)

I've identified and documented the following key components in `/workspace/answer.json`:

### 1. **Pod Lifecycle Manager** (`podWorkers`)
- **File**: `pkg/kubelet/pod_workers.go`
- Manages pod state transitions (Sync, Terminating, Terminated)
- Orchestrates pod updates and lifecycle operations

### 2. **Pod Lifecycle Event Generator** (`GenericPLEG`)
- **File**: `pkg/kubelet/pleg/generic.go`
- Discovers container state changes via periodic listing
- Generates pod lifecycle events for pod state monitoring

### 3. **Container Runtime Interface (CRI) Client** (`kubeGenericRuntimeManager`)
- **File**: `pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/kuberuntime_manager.go`
- Abstracts container runtime communication (Docker, containerd, CRI-O)
- Implements `SyncPod()` and container lifecycle operations

### 4. **Volume Manager** (`volumeManager`)
- **File**: `pkg/kubelet/volumemanager/volume_manager.go`
- Manages volume attachment and mounting lifecycle
- Maintains desired and actual state-of-world caches

### 5. **Device Plugin Manager** (`pluginManager`)
- **File**: `pkg/kubelet/pluginmanager/plugin_manager.go`
- Manages device plugin lifecycle and registration
- Coordinates plugin state synchronization

All components are confirmed to be owned by **sig-node** (as declared in `pkg/kubelet/OWNERS`), and work together to manage pod and container lifecycles in the kubelet.

It tracks plugin registration and deregistration through desired and actual state caches, similar to the volume manager. The `Run()` method starts the plugin watcher and reconciliation loops for managing plugin lifecycle.\\n\\n## Ownership\\n\\nAll these components are owned by sig-node as confirmed in `pkg/kubelet/OWNERS`:\\n- Approvers: sig-node-approvers\\n- Reviewers: sig-node-reviewers\\n- Labels: area/kubelet, sig/node\\n\\nThese five components form the core of kubelet's pod and container lifecycle management, working together to:\\n1.
